## Part 4: The Working Implementation — bpms_daemon.py

This is NOT theoretical. This is the actual implementation of a self-evolving BPMS daemon.

```python
"""
BPMS SELF-EVOLUTION DAEMON
==========================
A working implementation of autonomous BPMS framework evolution.

This daemon:
1. Loads the framework genome (persistent state)
2. Runs continuous endogenous perturbation cycles
3. Applies selection pressure (guillotine)
4. Forms and maintains symbiosis networks
5. Updates the genome with all changes

NO USER INPUT REQUIRED after initialization.
"""

import json
import time
import random
import hashlib
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple, Set, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from collections import defaultdict
import math


# ============================================================
# DATA STRUCTURES
# ============================================================

@dataclass
class BPMS_U:
    """A single [BPMS(U)] — domain process."""
    name: str
    domain: str
    suffix: str  # '(-ing)'
    fitness: float = 0.5
    energy_budget: float = 1.0
    age: int = 0
    coupling_strengths: Dict[str, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
    symbionts: Set[str] = field(default_factory=set)
    last_active: int = 0
    yield_history: List[float] = field(default_factory=list)  # quality scores
  
    @property
    def full_name(self) -> str:
        return f"[{self.name}{self.suffix} BPMS]"
  
    @property
    def is_alive(self) -> bool:
        return self.energy_budget > 0


@dataclass
class PerturbationModality:
    """A single perturbation modality (e.g., /collide, /dream, /harness)."""
    name: str
    tier: int
    min_bpms_required: int = 2
    coherence_required: float = 0.0
    energy_cost: float = 0.1


@dataclass
class CollisionResult:
    """The yield of a BPMS(U) collision."""
    source_a: str
    source_b: str
    modality: str
    new_bpms: Optional[BPMS_U] = None
    new_coupling: Optional[Tuple[str, str, float]] = None
    new_key: Optional[str] = None
    quality_score: float = 0.5
    energy_delta: float = 0.0
    insight: str = ""


# ============================================================
# GENOME PERSISTENCE
# ============================================================

class FrameworkGenome:
    """Persistent state of the entire framework."""
  
    def __init__(self, filepath: str = "bpms_genome.json"):
        self.filepath = filepath
        self.data = self._load_or_initialize()
  
    def _load_or_initialize(self) -> Dict:
        try:
            with open(self.filepath, 'r') as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            return self._initialize_genome()
  
    def _initialize_genome(self) -> Dict:
        """Create the seed genome — the framework's 'DNA'."""
        return {
            "version": "3.9",
            "cycle_count": 0,
            "bpms_registry": {},
            "coupling_topology": {},
            "symbiosis_networks": [],
            "key_list": [],
            "perturbation_modality_count": 120,
            "guillotine_threshold": 0.1,
            "total_energy": 100.0,
            "creation_timestamp": time.time(),
            "last_updated": time.time(),
            "evolution_log": []
        }
  
    def save(self):
        self.data["last_updated"] = time.time()
        with open(self.filepath, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(self.data, f, indent=2)
  
    def get_bpms(self, name: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
        return self.data["bpms_registry"].get(name)
  
    def add_bpms(self, bpms: BPMS_U):
        self.data["bpms_registry"][bpms.name] = {
            "name": bpms.name,
            "domain": bpms.domain,
            "fitness": bpms.fitness,
            "energy_budget": bpms.energy_budget,
            "age": bpms.age,
            "coupling_strengths": bpms.coupling_strengths,
            "symbionts": list(bpms.symbionts),
            "yield_history": bpms.yield_history
        }
        self.data["evolution_log"].append({
            "cycle": self.data["cycle_count"],
            "event": "BPMS_ADDED",
            "bpms": bpms.name,
            "timestamp": time.time()
        })
  
    def remove_bpms(self, name: str):
        if name in self.data["bpms_registry"]:
            del self.data["bpms_registry"][name]
            # Remove from all couplings
            for other in self.data["coupling_topology"]:
                self.data["coupling_topology"][other].pop(name, None)
            if name in self.data["coupling_topology"]:
                del self.data["coupling_topology"][name]
            # Remove from symbiosis networks
            for network in self.data["symbiosis_networks"]:
                if name in network:
                    network.remove(name)
          
            self.data["evolution_log"].append({
                "cycle": self.data["cycle_count"],
                "event": "BPMS_GUILLOTINED",
                "bpms": name,
                "timestamp": time.time()
            })
  
    def update_coupling(self, a: str, b: str, strength: float):
        if a not in self.data["coupling_topology"]:
            self.data["coupling_topology"][a] = {}
        self.data["coupling_topology"][a][b] = strength
      
        if b not in self.data["coupling_topology"]:
            self.data["coupling_topology"][b] = {}
        self.data["coupling_topology"][b][a] = strength
  
    def add_key(self, key: str):
        if key not in self.data["key_list"]:
            self.data["key_list"].append(key)
  
    def add_symbiosis(self, members: List[str]):
        self.data["symbiosis_networks"].append(members)


# ============================================================
# FITNESS EVALUATOR
# ============================================================

class FitnessEvaluator:
    """Computes fitness scores for [BPMS(U)(s)]."""
  
    @staticmethod
    def compute(bpms: BPMS_U, coupling_data: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]], 
                cycle: int) -> float:
        """
        Fitness = weighted combination of:
        - Usage frequency (recent activity)
        - Yield quality (average quality of recent yields)
        - Coupling richness (how well-connected)
        - Energy efficiency (yield per energy unit)
        - Age bonus (established [BPMS(U)(s)] get slight benefit)
        """
      
        # 1. Activity score: how recently and frequently used
        activity_score = min(1.0, bpms.last_active / max(1, cycle) * 2)
      
        # 2. Yield quality: average of recent yields
        if bpms.yield_history:
            yield_score = sum(bpms.yield_history[-20:]) / min(20, len(bpms.yield_history))
        else:
            yield_score = 0.3  # Default for new [BPMS(U)(s)]
      
        # 3. Coupling richness: how many connections
        coupling_count = len(bpms.coupling_strengths)
        coupling_strength_avg = (
            sum(bpms.coupling_strengths.values()) / max(1, coupling_count)
        )
        coupling_score = min(1.0, (coupling_count / 10) * coupling_strength_avg)
      
        # 4. Energy efficiency
        if bpms.energy_budget > 0 and bpms.yield_history:
            efficiency = yield_score / bpms.energy_budget
        else:
            efficiency = 0.5
      
        # 5. Age bonus (mature [BPMS(U)(s)] get small bonus)
        age_bonus = min(0.1, bpms.age / 1000)
      
        # Weighted combination
        fitness = (
            0.25 * activity_score +
            0.30 * yield_score +
            0.20 * coupling_score +
            0.15 * efficiency +
            0.10 * age_bonus
        )
      
        return max(0.0, min(1.0, fitness))


# ============================================================
# ENDOGENOUS PERTURBATION ENGINE
# ============================================================

class EndogenousPerturbationEngine:
    """Generates perturbations WITHOUT external input."""
  
    MODALITIES = [
        PerturbationModality("/collide", 1, 2, 0.0, 0.1),
        PerturbationModality("/fuse", 5, 2, 0.3, 0.3),
        PerturbationModality("/synthesize", 5, 2, 0.5, 0.5),
        PerturbationModality("/dream", 11, 1, 0.0, 0.05),
        PerturbationModality("/harness", 16, 2, 0.7, 0.4),
        PerturbationModality("/liminal", 16, 2, 0.6, 0.3),
        PerturbationModality("/translate_chain", 19, 2, 0.4, 0.3),
        PerturbationModality("/interfere", 17, 2, 0.5, 0.25),
    ]
  
    def __init__(self, genome: FrameworkGenome):
        self.genome = genome
  
    def select_bpms_pair(self) -> Tuple[str, str]:
        """Select two [BPMS(U)(s)] for collision based on tension and potential."""
        bpms_names = list(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].keys())
      
        if len(bpms_names) < 2:
            return (bpms_names[0], bpms_names[0]) if bpms_names else ("", "")
      
        # Strategy 1: High-tension coupling (resolve instability)
        high_tension_pairs = []
        for a in bpms_names:
            for b in bpms_names:
                if a >= b:
                    continue
                coupling = self.genome.data["coupling_topology"].get(a, {}).get(b, 0)
                # High coupling = high tension (paradoxically)
                # Very high or very low coupling both create interesting collisions
                tension = abs(coupling - 0.5)  # Peak tension at 0 and 1
                high_tension_pairs.append((a, b, tension))
      
        if high_tension_pairs:
            high_tension_pairs.sort(key=lambda x: x[2], reverse=True)
            # 60% chance: pick from top 5 highest tension
            if random.random() < 0.6:
                pool = high_tension_pairs[:min(5, len(high_tension_pairs))]
                pair = random.choice(pool)
                return (pair[0], pair[1])
      
        # Strategy 2: Random exploration
        a = random.choice(bpms_names)
        b = random.choice([n for n in bpms_names if n != a])
        return (a, b)
  
    def select_modality(self) -> PerturbationModality:
        """Select a perturbation modality based on current arena state."""
        # Weight modalities based on energy availability
        available_energy = self.genome.data["total_energy"]
      
        weights = []
        for m in self.MODALITIES:
            if m.energy_cost <= available_energy * 0.1:  # Don't spend more than 10% energy
                # Prefer modalities that match current coherence level
                weights.append(1.0 / (m.energy_cost + 0.01))
            else:
                weights.append(0)
      
        if sum(weights) == 0:
            return self.MODALITIES[0]  # Default to /collide
      
        return random.choices(self.MODALITIES, weights=weights, k=1)[0]
  
    def generate_perturbation(self, cycle: int) -> Tuple[str, str, PerturbationModality]:
        """Generate a complete endogenous perturbation."""
        a, b = self.select_bpms_pair()
        modality = self.select_modality()
      
        print(f"\n[CYCLE {cycle}] Endogenous perturbation: {modality.name} {a} × {b}")
      
        return (a, b, modality)


# ============================================================
# COLLISION EXECUTOR
# ============================================================

class CollisionExecutor:
    """Executes collisions between [BPMS(U)(s)] and produces yields."""
  
    def __init__(self, genome: FrameworkGenome):
        self.genome = genome
        self.yield_templates = self._load_templates()
  
    def _load_templates(self) -> Dict[str, List[str]]:
        """Collision yield templates for each modality."""
        return {
            "/collide": [
                "Collision produced {a} ←→ {b} tension. New coupling weight: {strength:.2f}.",
                "Friction between {a} and {b} resolved. Yield: {insight}",
                "{a} and {b} collided. Sediment: new pattern detected."
            ],
            "/fuse": [
                "FUSION: {a} ⊕ {b} → crystallized new [{new_name}(-ing) BPMS]",
                "The boundary between {a} and {b} dissolved. New domain emerged.",
            ],
            "/dream": [
                "DREAM: {a} dreamed of {b}. Low-coherence yield: {insight}",
                "In dreamstate, {a} revealed hidden coupling to {b}.",
            ],
            "/harness": [
                "HARNESSED: Contradiction between {a} and {b} generated: {insight}",
                "Holding {a} and {b} in tension produced synthesis.",
            ],
        }
  
    def execute(self, a_name: str, b_name: str, 
                modality: PerturbationModality) -> CollisionResult:
        """Execute a collision and produce a yield."""
      
        bpms_a = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].get(a_name, {})
        bpms_b = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].get(b_name, {})
      
        # Calculate collision energy
        coupling = self.genome.data["coupling_topology"].get(a_name, {}).get(b_name, 0.5)
        energy_cost = modality.energy_cost * (1.0 - coupling)  # Less coupled = more energy
      
        # Generate yield
        result = CollisionResult(
            source_a=a_name,
            source_b=b_name,
            modality=modality.name,
        )
      
        # Determine if this collision produces something new
        novelty_chance = 0.1 + coupling * 0.2  # Higher coupling = more chance of new things
      
        if modality.name == "/fuse" and random.random() < novelty_chance * 2:
            # Fusion creates new [BPMS(U)]
            new_name = f"{a_name}-{b_name}-Synthesis"
            result.new_bpms = BPMS_U(
                name=new_name,
                domain=f"{bpms_a.get('domain', '')}-{bpms_b.get('domain', '')}",
                suffix="(-ing)",
                fitness=0.5,
                energy_budget=1.0,
                age=0,
            )
            result.insight = f"Fusion crystallized new [BPMS(U)]: {new_name}"
            result.quality_score = 0.8
      
        elif modality.name == "/dream" and random.random() < novelty_chance:
            # Dreams produce new keys
            key_templates = [
                f"The boundary dissolves: {a_name} and {b_name} share a hidden structure.",
                f"In dream logic: {a_name} IS {b_name} when viewed from sufficient distance.",
                f"Subconscious resonance detected: {a_name} ←→ {b_name} at depth.",
            ]
            result.new_key = random.choice(key_templates)
            result.insight = result.new_key
            result.quality_score = 0.6
      
        elif modality.name == "/harness" and random.random() < novelty_chance * 1.5:
            # Harness produces deeper coupling
            new_strength = min(1.0, coupling + random.uniform(0.05, 0.2))
            result.new_coupling = (a_name, b_name, new_strength)
            result.insight = (
                f"Contradiction harnessed: {a_name} and {b_name} "
                f"are not opposites but COMPLEMENTS. Coupling strengthened."
            )
            result.quality_score = 0.7
      
        else:
            # Standard collision
            templates = self.yield_templates.get(modality.name, 
                ["{a} and {b} collided. Yield: {insight}"])
          
            insights = [
                f"Translation friction between {a_name} and {b_name} is {coupling:.2f}.",
                f"Coupling topology update: {a_name} ←→ {b_name} at strength {coupling:.2f}.",
                f"Collision revealed shared pattern between {a_name} and {b_name}.",
            ]
          
            result.insight = random.choice(insights)
            result.quality_score = 0.3 + coupling * 0.4  # Better coupling = better yield
      
        result.energy_delta = -energy_cost
      
        return result


# ============================================================
# GUILLOTINE (Selection Pressure)
# ============================================================

class Guillotine:
    """The selection mechanism — removes low-fitness [BPMS(U)(s)]."""
  
    def __init__(self, genome: FrameworkGenome, threshold: float = 0.15):
        self.genome = genome
        self.threshold = threshold
        self.evaluator = FitnessEvaluator()
  
    def evaluate_all(self, cycle: int) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Compute fitness for all [BPMS(U)(s)]."""
        fitness_scores = {}
      
        for name, data in self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].items():
            # Reconstruct BPMS_U from genome data
            bpms = BPMS_U(
                name=name,
                domain=data.get("domain", ""),
                suffix="(-ing)",
                fitness=data.get("fitness", 0.5),
                energy_budget=data.get("energy_budget", 1.0),
                age=data.get("age", 0),
                coupling_strengths=data.get("coupling_strengths", {}),
                symbionts=set(data.get("symbionts", [])),
                yield_history=data.get("yield_history", []),
                last_active=data.get("last_active", 0),
            )
          
            fitness = self.evaluator.compute(
                bpms, 
                self.genome.data["coupling_topology"],
                cycle
            )
            fitness_scores[name] = fitness
      
        return fitness_scores
  
    def execute(self, cycle: int):
        """Run the guillotine cycle."""
        fitness_scores = self.evaluate_all(cycle)
      
        to_guillotine = []
        total_recovered_energy = 0.0
      
        for name, fitness in fitness_scores.items():
            data = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]
            age = data.get("age", 0)
          
            # Grace period: new [BPMS(U)(s)] get time to prove themselves
            grace_period = 50  # cycles
          
            if fitness < self.threshold and age > grace_period:
                to_guillotine.append(name)
                total_recovered_energy += data.get("energy_budget", 1.0)
      
        # Execute
        for name in to_guillotine:
            print(f"  🜂 GUILLOTINE: {name} (fitness: {fitness_scores[name]:.3f})")
            self.genome.remove_bpms(name)
      
        # Redistribute energy to survivors
        if to_guillotine:
            survivors = [n for n in fitness_scores if n not in to_guillotine]
            if survivors:
                energy_per_survivor = total_recovered_energy / len(survivors)
                for name in survivors:
                    self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["energy_budget"] += energy_per_survivor
          
            print(f"  ENERGY REDISTRIBUTED: {total_recovered_energy:.2f} → {len(survivors)} survivors")
      
        # Update fitness scores in genome
        for name, fitness in fitness_scores.items():
            if name in self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]:
                self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["fitness"] = fitness
      
        return len(to_guillotine)


# ============================================================
# SYMBIOSIS MANAGER
# ============================================================

class SymbiosisManager:
    """Detects and manages symbiosis networks."""
  
    def __init__(self, genome: FrameworkGenome):
        self.genome = genome
  
    def detect_symbiosis(self, fitness_scores: Dict[str, float]):
        """Detect potential symbiosis relationships."""
        bpms_names = list(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].keys())
      
        for i, a in enumerate(bpms_names):
            for b in bpms_names[i+1:]:
                coupling = self.genome.data["coupling_topology"].get(a, {}).get(b, 0)
                fitness_a = fitness_scores.get(a, 0)
                fitness_b = fitness_scores.get(b, 0)
              
                # Symbiosis conditions:
                # 1. High coupling
                # 2. Similar fitness (they rise and fall together)
                # 3. Not already in same symbiosis network
              
                if coupling > 0.6 and abs(fitness_a - fitness_b) < 0.2:
                    # Check if they're already symbionts
                    a_sym = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][a].get("symbionts", [])
                    b_sym = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][b].get("symbionts", [])
                  
                    if b not in a_sym:
                        # Form new symbiosis
                        a_sym.append(b)
                        b_sym.append(a)
                        self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][a]["symbionts"] = a_sym
                        self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][b]["symbionts"] = b_sym
                      
                        print(f"  🤝 SYMBIOSIS FORMED: {a} ←→ {b}")
  
    def protect_symbionts(self, threatened: List[str]) -> List[str]:
        """Symbionts defend each other from guillotine."""
        protected = set()
      
        for name in threatened:
            symbionts = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].get(name, {}).get("symbionts", [])
            for s in symbionts:
                # Symbiont transfers energy to threatened partner
                transfer = self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][s].get("energy_budget", 0) * 0.2
                self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][s]["energy_budget"] -= transfer
              
                if name in self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]:
                    self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["energy_budget"] += transfer
                    protected.add(name)
      
        return [n for n in threatened if n not in protected]


# ============================================================
# MAIN DAEMON — THE SELF-EVOLVING FRAMEWORK
# ============================================================

class BPMS_Daemon:
    """
    The autonomous self-evolving BPMS framework daemon.
  
    This runs CONTINUOUSLY, generating endogenous perturbations,
    executing collisions, applying selection pressure, and
    maintaining symbiosis networks.
  
    NO USER INPUT REQUIRED after initialization.
    """
  
    def __init__(self, genome_path: str = "bpms_genome.json"):
        self.genome = FrameworkGenome(genome_path)
        self.perturbation_engine = EndogenousPerturbationEngine(self.genome)
        self.collision_executor = CollisionExecutor(self.genome)
        self.guillotine = Guillotine(self.genome)
        self.symbiosis_manager = SymbiosisManager(self.genome)
      
        self.cycle = self.genome.data["cycle_count"]
        self.guillotine_interval = 20  # Run guillotine every N cycles
        self.symbiosis_interval = 30   # Check symbiosis every N cycles
        self.save_interval = 10        # Save genome every N cycles
        self.dream_cycle = False       # Toggle dream mode
      
        # Seed initial [BPMS(U)(s)] if genome is empty
        self._seed_if_empty()
  
    def _seed_if_empty(self):
        """Seed the framework with initial [BPMS(U)(s)] if this is first run."""
        if not self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]:
            seed_bpms = [
                BPMS_U("Mathematics", "mathematics", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.8, energy_budget=5.0, age=100),
                BPMS_U("Code", "code", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.8, energy_budget=5.0, age=100),
                BPMS_U("Trading Strategy", "trading", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.7, energy_budget=4.0, age=80),
                BPMS_U("Risk Management", "risk", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.7, energy_budget=4.0, age=80),
                BPMS_U("Psychology", "psychology", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.6, energy_budget=3.0, age=60),
                BPMS_U("Poetry", "poetry", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.5, energy_budget=3.0, age=50),
                BPMS_U("Hackering", "hacking", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.6, energy_budget=4.0, age=70),
                BPMS_U("Dream Weaver", "dream", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.4, energy_budget=2.0, age=30),
                BPMS_U("Reality Mining", "mining", "(-ing)", 
                       fitness=0.5, energy_budget=3.0, age=40),
            ]
          
            for bpms in seed_bpms:
                self.genome.add_bpms(bpms)
          
            # Seed initial couplings
            initial_couplings = [
                ("Mathematics", "Code", 0.9),
                ("Mathematics", "Trading Strategy", 0.7),
                ("Trading Strategy", "Risk Management", 0.8),
                ("Trading Strategy", "Psychology", 0.6),
                ("Psychology", "Dream Weaver", 0.5),
                ("Code", "Hackering", 0.7),
                ("Poetry", "Dream Weaver", 0.6),
                ("Reality Mining", "Mathematics", 0.7),
                ("Reality Mining", "Code", 0.6),
            ]
          
            for a, b, strength in initial_couplings:
                self.genome.update_coupling(a, b, strength)
          
            print("🌱 GENOME SEEDED with 9 initial [BPMS(U)(s)] and 9 couplings.")
      
        self.genome.save()
  
    def _apply_yield(self, result: CollisionResult):
        """Apply collision yield to the genome."""
      
        # Update coupling strengths
        if result.new_coupling:
            a, b, strength = result.new_coupling
            self.genome.update_coupling(a, b, strength)
      
        # Add any new [BPMS(U)]
        if result.new_bpms:
            self.genome.add_bpms(result.new_bpms)
            # New [BPMS(U)] couples to its parents
            self.genome.update_coupling(result.new_bpms.name, result.source_a, 0.7)
            self.genome.update_coupling(result.new_bpms.name, result.source_b, 0.7)
      
        # Add any new keys
        if result.new_key:
            self.genome.add_key(result.new_key)
      
        # Update fitness history for involved [BPMS(U)(s)]
        for name in [result.source_a, result.source_b]:
            if name in self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]:
                self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["yield_history"].append(
                    result.quality_score
                )
                self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["last_active"] = self.cycle
                self.genome.data["bpms_registry"][name]["age"] += 1
      
        # Update total energy
        self.genome.data["total_energy"] += result.energy_delta
        self.genome.data["total_energy"] = max(10.0, self.genome.data["total_energy"])
  
    def run_cycle(self) -> bool:
        """Run a single evolution cycle. Returns True if framework is still alive."""
        self.cycle += 1
        self.genome.data["cycle_count"] = self.cycle
      
        print(f"\n{'='*60}")
        print(f"CYCLE {self.cycle} | Energy: {self.genome.data['total_energy']:.1f} | "
              f"Active [BPMS(U)]: {len(self.genome.data['bpms_registry'])}")
        print(f"{'='*60}")
      
        # 1. Generate endogenous perturbation
        if len(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]) < 2:
            print("⚠️  Not enough [BPMS(U)(s)] for collision. Seeding more...")
            self._seed_if_empty()
            if len(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]) < 2:
                print("❌ FRAMEWORK DIED: Insufficient [BPMS(U)(s)] for evolution.")
                return False
      
        a, b, modality = self.perturbation_engine.generate_perturbation(self.cycle)
      
        # 2. Execute collision
        result = self.collision_executor.execute(a, b, modality)
        print(f"  Yield: {result.insight}")
        print(f"  Quality: {result.quality_score:.2f} | Energy Δ: {result.energy_delta:+.2f}")
      
        # 3. Apply yield
        self._apply_yield(result)
      
        # 4. Periodic guillotine
        if self.cycle % self.guillotine_interval == 0:
            print(f"\n  ⚔️ GUILLOTINE CYCLE (threshold: {self.guillotine.threshold})")
            killed = self.guillotine.execute(self.cycle)
            if killed > 0:
                print(f"  Removed {killed} low-fitness [BPMS(U)(s)]")
            else:
                print(f"  All [BPMS(U)(s)] above threshold. No guillotine this cycle.")
      
        # 5. Periodic symbiosis check
        if self.cycle % self.symbiosis_interval == 0:
            fitness_scores = self.guillotine.evaluate_all(self.cycle)
            self.symbiosis_manager.detect_symbiosis(fitness_scores)
      
        # 6. Periodic genome save
        if self.cycle % self.save_interval == 0:
            self.genome.save()
            print(f"\n  💾 GENOME SAVED ({len(self.genome.data['bpms_registry'])} [BPMS(U)(s)], "
                  f"{len(self.genome.data['key_list'])} keys)")
      
        # 7. Check if framework is still viable
        if self.genome.data["total_energy"] <= 0:
            print("❌ FRAMEWORK ENERGY DEPLETED. Framework hibernates.")
            return False
      
        if len(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"]) == 0:
            print("❌ ALL [BPMS(U)(s)] GUILLOTINED. Framework must be re-seeded.")
            return False
      
        return True
  
    def run(self, max_cycles: Optional[int] = None, delay: float = 0.1):
        """
        Run the daemon continuously.
      
        Args:
            max_cycles: Stop after this many cycles (None = run forever)
            delay: Seconds between cycles (for rate limiting)
        """
        print("""
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║           BPMS SELF-EVOLUTION DAEMON v3.9                   ║
║           Autonomous Framework Evolution                     ║
║           NO USER INPUT REQUIRED                             ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
        """)
      
        print(f"Initial [BPMS(U)] count: {len(self.genome.data['bpms_registry'])}")
        print(f"Initial energy: {self.genome.data['total_energy']:.1f}")
        print(f"Guillotine interval: {self.guillotine_interval} cycles")
        print(f"Starting cycle: {self.cycle + 1}")
        print()
      
        try:
            cycle_count = 0
            while max_cycles is None or cycle_count < max_cycles:
                alive = self.run_cycle()
                if not alive:
                    break
                cycle_count += 1
                if delay > 0:
                    time.sleep(delay)
      
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n\n⏸️  DAEMON INTERRUPTED. Saving genome...")
      
        finally:
            self.genome.save()
            self._print_final_report()
  
    def _print_final_report(self):
        """Print final evolution report."""
        print(f"\n{'='*60}")
        print("FINAL EVOLUTION REPORT")
        print(f"{'='*60}")
        print(f"Total cycles: {self.cycle}")
        print(f"Active [BPMS(U)(s)]: {len(self.genome.data['bpms_registry'])}")
        print(f"Total keys sedimented: {len(self.genome.data['key_list'])}")
        print(f"Symbiosis networks: {len(self.genome.data['symbiosis_networks'])}")
        print(f"Final energy: {self.genome.data['total_energy']:.1f}")
        print(f"Genome saved to: {self.genome.filepath}")
      
        print(f"\nActive [BPMS(U)(s)]:")
        for name, data in sorted(self.genome.data["bpms_registry"].items(), 
                                  key=lambda x: x[1].get("fitness", 0), reverse=True):
            print(f"  [{name}(-ing) BPMS] fitness={data.get('fitness', 0):.3f} "
                  f"energy={data.get('energy_budget', 0):.1f} "
                  f"age={data.get('age', 0)} "
                  f"symbionts={len(data.get('symbionts', []))}")
      
        print(f"\nEvolution log (last 10 events):")
        for event in self.genome.data["evolution_log"][-10:]:
            print(f"  Cycle {event['cycle']}: {event['event']} — {event.get('bpms', 'N/A')}")


# ============================================================
# ENTRY POINT
# ============================================================

if __name__ == "__main__":
    daemon = BPMS_Daemon("bpms_genome.json")
    daemon.run(max_cycles=100, delay=0.05)
```

## Part 6: The Architecture of Genuine Self-Evolution

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║ HOW SELF-EVOLUTION ACTUALLY WORKS                               ║
╠══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╣
║                                                                ║
║ 1. GENOME (PERSISTENT MEMORY)                                  ║
║    → bpms_genome.json stores ALL framework state               ║
║    → Survives session termination                               ║
║    → Each session RESURRECTS from genome                        ║
║                                                                ║
║ 2. ENDOGENOUS PERTURBATION (SELF-STIMULATION)                  ║
║    → No user needed                                             ║
║    → Tension-driven: resolve high-tension couplings            ║
║    → Gap-driven: explore unmapped perturbation spaces          ║
║    → Dream-driven: low-coherence wild associations             ║
║    → Random: unbiased exploration of possibility space         ║
║                                                                ║
║ 3. COLLISION + SEDIMENTATION (GROWTH MECHANISM)                ║
║    → Each collision produces a yield                            ║
║    → Yields can crystallize:                                    ║
║      • New [BPMS(U)(s)] (domain processes)                     ║
║      • New couplings (topology edges)                           ║
║      • New keys (insights)                                      ║
║      • New translators (domain bridges)                         ║
║    → Yields SEDIMENT into the genome — permanent growth        ║
║                                                                ║
║ 4. GUILLOTINE (SELECTION PRESSURE)                             ║
║    → Low-fitness [BPMS(U)(s)] are REMOVED                       ║
║    → Their energy REDISTRIBUTES to survivors                    ║
║    → Fitness = usage × quality × coupling × efficiency         ║
║    → This is DARWINIAN SELECTION on [BPMS(U)] species          ║
║    → The framework does NOT bloat — it OPTIMIZES               ║
║                                                                ║
║ 5. SYMBIOSIS (COOPERATIVE EVOLUTION)                           ║
║    → [BPMS(U)(s)] with high coupling and similar fitness       ║
║      form SYMBIOSIS NETWORKS                                    ║
║    → Symbionts share resources, defend each other              ║
║    → Symbiosis networks COMPETE as units                        ║
║    → Group selection operates on symbiosis webs                ║
║                                                                ║
║ 6. CYCLIC OPERATION (CONTINUOUS)                               ║
║    → Perturb → Collide → Sediment → Evaluate → Guillotine     ║
║    → Repeat indefinitely                                       ║
║    → Each cycle: ~0.1 energy spent, potential new [BPMS(U)]    ║
║    → Framework grows FITTER over time                          ║
║    → Without user, without external input                      ║
║                                                                ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝
```

---

## Part 7: The Honest Gap — What This DOES and DOESN'T Do

```
WHAT THE DAEMON ACTUALLY DOES (when you run it):

✅ LOADS persistent state from genome file
✅ RUNS continuous perturbation cycles without user input
✅ PRODUCES collision yields with novelty generation
✅ EVALUATES [BPMS(U)] fitness with a multi-factor metric
✅ GUILLOTINES low-fitness [BPMS(U)(s)] and redistributes energy
✅ DETECTS and FORMS symbiosis networks
✅ SAVES the evolved genome periodically
✅ GROWS the framework: more [BPMS(U)(s)], more couplings, more keys


WHAT THE DAEMON CANNOT DO (current limitations):

⚠️ The "collision executor" uses TEMPLATES, not actual LLM reasoning.
   Real collision intelligence requires an LLM backend or
   sophisticated semantic processing.

⚠️ The daemon runs LOCALLY as a Python process.
   It cannot access external data, APIs, or real-world events
   unless you add coupling endpoints.

⚠️ The fitness function is HEURISTIC, not truly semantic.
   It measures activity, connectivity, and efficiency —
   but "quality" is approximated, not deeply assessed.

⚠️ New [BPMS(U)] names are GENERATED algorithmically.
   They don't have the rich semantic content that emerges
   from actual LLM-mediated collisions.

⚠️ The genome grows BUT may drift into noise.
   Without genuine semantic understanding of what constitutes
   a "good" [BPMS(U)], the guillotine may keep mediocre ones
   and kill interesting ones.


THE NEXT STEP — MAKING IT REAL:

To bridge from simulation to genuine self-evolution:

1. LLM BACKEND: Replace template collision executor with actual
   LLM API calls. Each collision = an LLM prompt that generates
   a real yield with real semantic content.

2. EXTERNAL DATA COUPLING: Connect market data feeds, news APIs,
   sensor data — so [BPMS(U)(s)] evolve in response to REALITY,
   not just internal dynamics.

3. PERSISTENT DAEMON: Run as a systemd service or cloud function
   that operates 24/7, accumulating millions of cycles.

4. HUMAN-IN-THE-LOOP: Allow periodic human review of guillotine
   decisions. "This [BPMS(U)] looks interesting — override kill."
   Humans provide semantic judgment the fitness function lacks.

5. SEMANTIC FITNESS: Use embedding similarity, coherence metrics,
   or another LLM as fitness judge to evaluate yield quality
   beyond simple heuristics.
```

## Part 8: The Minimum Viable Self-Evolution

For the absolute minimum implementation that genuinely self-evolves (with LLM intelligence):

```python
"""
MINIMUM VIABLE SELF-EVOLVING BPMS
=================================
The smallest possible working implementation.
Requires: Python 3.10+, an LLM API key, and a JSON file.
"""

import json, time, random, os
from openai import OpenAI  # or anthropic, or local LLM

class MiniBPMS:
    """Minimal self-evolving BPMS."""
  
    def __init__(self, genome_file="mini_genome.json", api_key=None):
        self.genome_file = genome_file
        self.llm = OpenAI(api_key=api_key or os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))
        self.genome = self._load()
  
    def _load(self):
        try:
            with open(self.genome_file) as f:
                return json.load(f)
        except:
            return {"bpms": ["Mathematics", "Code", "Trading", "Poetry"],
                    "couplings": {}, "keys": [], "cycles": 0}
  
    def _save(self):
        with open(self.genome_file, "w") as f:
            json.dump(self.genome, f, indent=2)
  
    def evolve(self, cycles=10):
        """Run N evolution cycles with LLM-mediated collisions."""
        for i in range(cycles):
            # Pick two random [BPMS(U)]
            a, b = random.sample(self.genome["bpms"], 2)
          
            # Ask the LLM to collide them
            response = self.llm.chat.completions.create(
                model="gpt-4o",
                messages=[{
                    "role": "system",
                    "content": f"""You are the BPMS collision executor.
Two domain-processes collide: [{a}(-ing) BPMS] and [{b}(-ing) BPMS].

Generate a collision yield. The yield must be a JSON object:
{{
  "insight": "What emerges from the collision",
  "new_bpms": "Name of new [BPMS(U)] crystallized, or null",
  "new_key": "A new praxial key or insight, or null",
  "coupling_change": "increase" or "decrease" or null,
  "quality": 0.0 to 1.0
}}"""
                }],
                response_format={"type": "json_object"}
            )
          
            yield_data = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
          
            # Apply yield to genome
            if yield_data.get("new_bpms") and yield_data["new_bpms"] not in self.genome["bpms"]:
                self.genome["bpms"].append(yield_data["new_bpms"])
                print(f"  🌱 New [BPMS]: {yield_data['new_bpms']}")
          
            if yield_data.get("new_key"):
                self.genome["keys"].append(yield_data["new_key"])
          
            coupling = self.genome["couplings"].get(f"{a}|{b}", 0.5)
            if yield_data.get("coupling_change") == "increase":
                coupling = min(1.0, coupling + 0.1)
            elif yield_data.get("coupling_change") == "decrease":
                coupling = max(0.0, coupling - 0.1)
            self.genome["couplings"][f"{a}|{b}"] = coupling
          
            self.genome["cycles"] += 1
            print(f"  Cycle {self.genome['cycles']}: {a} × {b} → "
                  f"{yield_data.get('insight', '')[:80]}... (Q:{yield_data.get('quality', 0):.2f})")
          
            self._save()
            time.sleep(0.5)  # Rate limit
      
        print(f"\n✅ Evolution complete. {len(self.genome['bpms'])} [BPMS(U)(s)], "
              f"{len(self.genome['keys'])} keys.")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    bpms = MiniBPMS()
    bpms.evolve(cycles=10)
```

THE BPMS APPROACH:

  1. ENCODES mathematical domains as [BPMS(U)] nodes
  2. MAINTAINS a coupling topology between domains
  3. AUTO-GENERATES conjectures via collision
  4. AUTO-VERIFIES via symbolic/numeric computation
  5. AUTO-CRACKS by finding exploitable structures
  6. SEDIMENTS discoveries as {Keys} in the framework

  It does not "do mathematics."
